<span style="background-color:#000000; font-weight:700">
<font color="#00FF00" face="Arial" size="4">“The Gospel is not a call to repentance, or to amendment of our 
			ways, to make restitution for past sins, or to promise to do better 
			in the future. These things are proper in their place, but they do 
			not constitute the Gospel; for the Gospel is not good advice to be 
			obeyed, it is good news to be believed. Do not make the mistake then 
			of thinking that the Gospel is a call to duty or a call to 
			reformation, a call to better your condition, to behave yourself in 
			a more perfect way than you have been doing in the past …</font></span><o:p></o:p></p>
<p style="border:medium none;mso-border-bottom-alt:dotted windowtext 3.0pt;padding:
0in;mso-padding-alt:0in 0in 1.0pt 0in; ">
<span style="background-color:#000000; font-weight:700">
<font color="#00FF00" face="Arial" size="4">Nor is the Gospel a demand that you give up the world, that you 
			<a href="Basics/do_i_have_to_give_up_sin_to_be_saved.htm">give 
			up your sins</a>, that you break off bad habits, and try to cultivate 
			good ones. You may do all these things, and yet never believe the 
			Gospel and consequently never be saved at all.”</font></span><o:p></o:p></p>

away from us<span lang="en-us"> . . . </span>Yes, you may feel

        Church of Hammond will become a great church when we stop saying, <br/>
		'He 
        has sinned' and 'She has sinned' and we start saying '<a href="http://www.jesusisprecious.org/fundamentals/we_have_sinned.htm">WE 
        HAVE SINNED!</a>'”</span></i></font></b></span><font color="#ffffff" face="Verdana" size="2"><br/>—<span lang="en-us" style="background-color: #000000">SOURCE: 
        (<i><a href="http://www.jesus-is-savior.com/Books,%20Tracts%20&amp;%20Preaching/Printed%20Books/Dr%20Jack%20Hyles/Types/types-chap_2.htm">Treatment 
        Of The Fallen</a></i>, from the life-changing book by Dr. Jack Hyles 
        (1926-2001), <br/><i>
<a href="Books,%20Tracts%20&amp;%20Preaching/Printed%20Books/Dr%20Jack%20Hyles/how_to_treat_different_types_of_church_members.htm">HOW TO TREAT DIFFERENT TYPES OF CHURCH MEMBERS</a></i>)</span></font><font color="#FFFFFF" face="Verdana"><font size="2">.</font></font></p>
<p align="center"><b><i><span lang="en-us">
<font color="#FF0000" face="Verdana" size="5">
<span style="background-color: #000000">Psalms 106:6, “</span></font><span style="background-color: #000000"><font color="#FFFFFF" face="Verdana" size="5"><u>We 
      have sinned</u></font></span><font color="#FF0000" face="Verdana" size="5"><span style="background-color: #000000"> 
      with our fathers, <br/>
      we have committed iniquity, we have done wickedly.”</span></font></span></i></b></p>
